Turner & Townsend and CBRE work together to provide clients with the premier program, project and cost management offering in markets around the world. 

Turner & Townsend
 is seeking an experienced 
Director of Project Controls
 to lead cost, schedule, and risk management for a large-scale data center construction program in 
Beaver County, PA
, while supporting major client accounts and broader business initiatives. This is a senior leadership role responsible for establishing and overseeing robust project controls processes, ensuring accurate forecasting, reporting, and governance across all phases of delivery.
The Director will partner with project leadership, contractors, and stakeholders to maintain transparency, mitigate risks, and drive performance against budget and schedule targets. You will lead project controls teams, ensure best practices are implemented, and act as a trusted advisor to clients.

Responsibilities
Establish and execute the strategic direction for project controls, including cost, schedule, and risk management, for a large-scale data center program.
Develop and implement governance frameworks, reporting protocols, and project controls processes to ensure accuracy and compliance.
Oversee budgeting, forecasting, earned value analysis, variance reporting, and lifecycle cost estimating; validate estimates and track actuals against forecasts.
Lead development and integration of detailed CPM schedules (Primavera P6/MS Project) across design, procurement, construction, and commissioning; monitor critical path and implement recovery plans.
Define and manage risk registers; lead risk workshops, establish mitigation strategies, and coordinate contingency planning, including Monte Carlo analyses.
Manage change control processes, including evaluation of scope changes, impact analysis, and cost reduction initiatives.
Prepare executive-level dashboards, gateway documentation, and reports for senior leadership, highlighting performance, risks, and corrective actions.
Ensure alignment on cost and schedule objectives through collaboration with project managers, finance teams, and contractors; support client reporting and governance meetings.
Drive data integrity and reporting accuracy across all phases; utilize project controls tools and platforms (e.g., Primavera P6, MS Project, cost systems).
Develop and maintain protocols for performance measurement, forecasting, trending, and progress reporting against project baselines.
Lead and mentor a high-performing project controls team; provide clear direction, conduct performance reviews, and foster a culture of accountability and continuous improvement.
Motivate the team through regular meetings, clear goals, and quality assurance of deliverables; ensure integration of intake, cost, and scheduling processes for end-to-end project controls.
Act as a key liaison with internal and external stakeholders; review implementation plans, claims resolution recommendations, and recovery strategies.
Support business initiatives by identifying opportunities for process improvement, knowledge sharing, and integration of best practices across projects.
SOX control responsibilities may be part of this role, which are to be adhered to where applicable.

Bachelor’s degree in Construction Management, Quantity Surveying, Engineering, Finance, or a related field; graduate degree preferred.
12+ years of experience in project controls, cost management, and scheduling for large-scale construction programs (data center or mission-critical preferred), including 2+ years leading high-performing project controls teams in a consulting environment.
Proven ability to manage complex budgets, schedules, and risk for multi-million-dollar projects; experience establishing and monitoring baselines and performance metrics.
Expertise in cost forecasting, earned value management (EVM), risk analysis, and change management; strong knowledge of multiple contract delivery methods.
Demonstrated success in implementing and managing integrated project controls systems, including financial and scheduling controls, for major capital projects.
Proficiency in Primavera P6, MS Project, and cost management systems; advanced Excel skills for data analysis and reporting.
Professional certifications such as CCP, PSP, PMP, or equivalent highly desirable.
Excellent analytical, leadership, and communication skills; ability to interpret complex data, influence stakeholders, and drive performance.
Knowledge of industry standards, regulatory requirements, and compliance frameworks relevant to large-scale construction programs.

*On-site presence and requirements may change depending on our client's needs.

Drive data integrity and reporting accuracy across all phases; utilize project controls tools and platforms (e.g., Primavera P6, MS Project, cost systems).
Develop and maintain protocols for performance measurement, forecasting, trending, and progress reporting against project baselines.
Lead and mentor a high-performing project controls team; provide clear direction, conduct performance reviews, and foster a culture of accountability and continuous improvement.
Motivate the team through regular meetings, clear goals, and quality assurance of deliverables; ensure integration of intake, cost, and scheduling processes for end-to-end project controls.
Act as a key liaison with internal and external stakeholders; review implementation plans, claims resolution recommendations, and recovery strategies.
Support business initiatives by identifying opportunities for process improvement, knowledge sharing, and integration of best practices across projects.
SOX control responsibilities may be part of this role, which are to be adhered to where applicable.

Bachelor’s degree in Construction Management, Quantity Surveying, Engineering, Finance, or a related field; graduate degree preferred.
12+ years of experience in project controls, cost management, and scheduling for large-scale construction programs (data center or mission-critical preferred), including 2+ years leading high-performing project controls teams in a consulting environment.
Proven ability to manage complex budgets, schedules, and risk for multi-million-dollar projects; experience establishing and monitoring baselines and performance metrics.
Expertise in cost forecasting, earned value management (EVM), risk analysis, and change management; strong knowledge of multiple contract delivery methods.
Demonstrated success in implementing and managing integrated project controls systems, including financial and scheduling controls, for major capital projects.
Proficiency in Primavera P6, MS Project, and cost management systems; advanced Excel skills for data analysis and reporting.
Professional certifications such as CCP, PSP, PMP, or equivalent highly desirable.
Excellent analytical, leadership, and communication skills; ability to interpret complex data, influence stakeholders, and drive performance.
Knowledge of industry standards, regulatory requirements, and compliance frameworks relevant to large-scale construction programs.

*On-site presence and requirements may change depending on our client's needs.

Senior Scheduler - CQV
Richmond, Virginia, US · Posted: 2026-06-24T20:08:45.466Z
Comp: Not listed
Job description
Turner & Townsend is a global professional services company with over 22,000 people in more than 60 countries. 
Working with our clients across real estate, infrastructure, energy and natural resources, we transform together delivering outcomes that improve people’s lives. Working in partnership makes it possible to deliver the world’s most impactful projects and programmes as we turn challenge into opportunity and complexity into success. 
Our capabilities include programme, project, cost, asset and commercial management, controls and performance, procurement and supply chain, net zero and digital solutions. 
We are majority-owned by CBRE Group, Inc., the world’s largest commercial real estate services and investment firm, with our partners holding a significant minority interest. Turner & Townsend and CBRE work together to provide clients with the premier programme, project and cost management offering in markets around the world. 

Turner & Townsend
 is seeking an experienced 
Senior CQV Scheduler
 to join our team to support scheduling as a project controls function on a large-scale project. The ideal individual will have a proven track record of successfully delivering construction project control services.   
Responsibilities:  
Develop, monitor and update owners' Project Integrated Master Schedule (IMS).  
Establish the schedule management program and deliverables to be used on large scale capital programs.  
Interface with project stakeholders as trusted advisors to provide guidance and recommendations for the project.  
Prepare baseline schedules and schedule basis documents for approval by project teams.  
Conduct schedule of resource loading and leveling.  
Consolidate contractors schedule to incorporate into IMS.  
Assess impacts on the critical path and near-critical activities and report to the project team.  
Monitor schedule deviations and variances and assist in the development of alternative methods for corrective action.  
Apply EVM methodology to measure project progress.  
Review schedules with project team members on a regular basis to ensure that accurate and timely data is incorporated into the schedule.  
Prepare and provide schedule progress reports, trending charts, and schedule analysis on a periodic basis.  
Maintain record of scope changes, trends and variances that potentially affect schedule performance.  
Assure the credibility of the information contained in the schedule.  
Maintain liaison with clients and other consultants at all projects stages.  
SOX control responsibilities may be part of this role, which are to be adhered to where applicable. 
Project/Program specifications: 
Develop and manage detailed CQV (Commissioning, Qualification, and Validation) schedules for complex life sciences construction projects, ensuring alignment with project milestones and regulatory requirements.
Collaborate with cross-functional teams including engineering, construction, and quality to integrate CQV activities into overall project timelines.
Monitor progress of CQV tasks, identify potential delays, and proactively implement mitigation strategies to keep projects on track.
Utilize scheduling tools such as Primavera P6 or MS Project to create and maintain accurate schedules and reports.
Support resource planning and allocation for CQV activities across multiple concurrent projects.
Ensure compliance with GMP (Good Manufacturing Practices) and other regulatory standards throughout the CQV lifecycle.
Provide regular updates and reports to project stakeholders, highlighting key risks, dependencies, and progress metrics.
Experience in biotech, pharmaceutical, or life sciences facility construction is required; familiarity with cleanroom environments and process equipment is a plus.

Bachelor’s degree in construction management, cost management, quantity surveying, engineering or field related to construction. 
Minimum 5-7 years of applicable experience. 
Direct experience working on teams within a complex matrix environment.  
Expertise using Primavera P6.  
Excellent communication skills.  

*On-site presence and requirements may change depending on our clients' needs.*

Turner & Townsend is a global professional services company with over 22,000 people in more than 60 countries.

Turner & Townsend 
is seeking a 
Senior Construction Scheduler 
to work with our team in 
West Memphis
, 
AR
 and a leading technology client on a large-scale data center construction program.
The Senior Scheduler should have experience working with cross-functional teams and stakeholders to plan, develop and execute construction schedules for mission critical facilities. This includes new-builds and retrofits to existing /operating facilities.
The ideal candidate should have an excellent understanding of scheduling best practices, resource & cost loaded scheduling, overall construction project controls as well as the interpersonal skills to be able to work closely with the internal stakeholders of the project team on a daily basis.
The Senior Scheduler will take responsibility for end to end service delivery and to act as key, day to day client interface, ensuring that client objectives are met through the delivery of a value added service. To be successful in this role you must have great communication skills and be comfortable operating in a client-facing role.
Responsibilities:
Regular travel to construction site is expected.
Effectively work with Stakeholders, Clients, Contractors and Sub Contractors on a daily basis.
Develop and maintain a detailed construction program schedule using Primavera P6 and Tableau for multi-project environments.
Ensure that schedule related data from vendors, suppliers, engineering and construction contractors of actual projects is provided as feedback into the planning and scheduling systems.
Implement Project Planning & Scheduling strategy, plans and procedures, reflecting both Company and contractor roles, responsibilities and expectations.
Actively work with project managers, construction firms and subcontractor firms as necessary to maintain schedule integrity.
Provide interface and quality assurance to Project functional groups and contractors regarding the tracking and reporting of schedule performance.
Ability to coordinate & organize multiple sources of schedule inputs/performance data into a master schedule platform and deliver project/program status reports as required.
Prepare and update progress reports as required by the client, including the Integrated Planning / Scheduling contribution to the monthly project report and specific reports / presentations.
Produce high level and 1, 3, 6 month look ahead from P6 for reporting.
Perform probabilistic analysis on integrated schedules and contractor schedules.
Actively monitor and communicate any possible project issues that could delay the schedule.
Conduct the required project schedule analysis, critical path analysis and schedule risk analysis for the project as a whole.
Analyze deviations from the baseline in the Project Master schedule highlighting bottlenecks / delays and propose corrective actions, and highlight the overall schedule impact of any variance / change order.
SOX control responsibilities may be part of this role, which are to be adhered to where applicable. 

Experience working in mission critical environments is preferred including commissioning activities.
Construction experience- i.e. “boots on the ground.” This is site-level construction experience who knows the construction process.
Understanding of best practice relating to the delivery of a construction program is required.
Extensive experience creating and managing large-scale construction schedules in Primavera P6.
A background in Project Controls is beneficial.
Familiarity with construction drawings, specifications and construction sequencing is required.
Being able to work independently is crucial.
Capable of producing detailed concept level schedules from limited project information. Identifying major phases through that timeline and be able to determine and discuss dependencies.
Working closely with various disciplines in project teams to ensure the accuracy and completeness of the schedules produced without compromising your independence as a scheduler so you are in a position to advise project management on issues requiring judgment.
Knowledge of system start-up sequences and major dependencies.
Able to convert data into Tableau reports and graphics.
Excellent collaboration and communication skills are required.
BS Degree in Engineering or Business or related field; or demonstrated equivalent and related experience.
PSP certification by AACE in planning/scheduling is beneficial.
EIT certification Preferred.

Project Overview:
 
Bechtel is partnering with NextDecade to support their vision to provide the world access to lower carbon intensive energy with their Rio Grande LNG (RGLNG) project in Brownsville, Texas. RGLNG is a natural gas liquefaction and export terminal situated on a 984-acre site on the banks of the Brownsville ship channel. The first phase of the RGLNG project consists of three liquefaction trains, two storage tanks and one marine berth. At full capacity, the five-train facility will have a production capacity of 27 million tonnes per annum (MTPA). Brownsville, Texas is a city known for its diverse history, tradition, and rich culture. Located in the southernmost region in the beautiful state of Texas, lays Brownsville a rich, tropical oasis bordering the Rio Grande River and near the shores of the Gulf of Mexico. Brownsville embraces innovation, looks forward to the future and beyond!
Job Summary:
 
In this role, you will lead, implement, and maintain global construction field welding programs and provide specialized welding engineering support. You will manage, inspect, and monitor the welding test lab, the rod room, the weld heat treatment program, and the laboratory quality plan. Your technical advice will help ensure defects, behaviors, and other issues are rectified prior to final inspection.
 #LI-BH1
Major Responsibilities:
 
Coordinates work activities for Project Field Engineer and the Lead Field Welding engineer in implementing the site welding program on medium projects 
Implements and maintains Bechtel Field Welding program for all welding operations.  
Provides technical assistance to field superintendents and crafts.  
Ensures that all supervision and craft personnel involved in welding operations are educated and aware of applicable code and project requirements.  
Reviews site Welding, PWHT and NDE subcontractor documentation of daily work for technical accuracy 
Performs Visual and other examination methods in accordance with project developed procedures and standards. 
Implements Design Automation deliverables 
Education and Experience Requirements:
 
Requires bachelor's degree (or international equivalent) and 5-8 years of relevant experience or 9-12 years of relevant work experience​
Required Knowledge and Skills:
 
Candidates should be self-starters, highly motivated, requiring little supervision, and able to work well in a team environment.
The candidate should have a good working knowledge of current design codes and standards such as UPC, IBC, SMACNA, ASME, AWS, and NFPA.
The candidate should have a good working knowledge of welding technical and practical applications such as SMAW, GTAW, GMAW STT.
The candidate should have a good working knowledge of Preheat/Post Weld Heat Treatments, equipment, and consumables.
Excellent oral and written communication skills.
A sound knowledge base of environmental, safety and health compliance standards required on government projects.

Mechanical/Piping system construction installation and inspection experience.
Working knowledge of mechanical/piping engineering principles in the design and installation of structures, systems, and components.
Strong ability to read, understand and interpret structural/mechanical/piping/electrical construction drawings.
Technical knowledge of a specialized engineering discipline, cost, scheduling and contracts administration relating to the construction of heavy industrial or commercial complexes.
Strong understanding of module assembly, completion walk-downs, testing, punch list management, turn over packages and routine interface with Start-Up.
Knowledge of requirements for Lock Out Tag Out for safety.
Computer literate in word processing, spreadsheet, and database applications in accordance with current Bechtel standards.
Working knowledge of Bechtel Construction automation systems (e.g., TeamWorks, InfoWorks, WITS, etc).
Ability to interface with diverse construction disciplines as well as all levels of management.

Recent Bechtel experience as a Welding/Mechanical/Piping Field Engineer or Lead Welding/Mechanical/Piping Field Engineer at a large EPC Project.
Working knowledge of the Bechtel Standard Work Processes Procedures (*SWPPs) and the related Bechtel Standard application Programs (BSAPs) utilized by Construction

Senior Scheduler - Data Center Construction

Job description
Turner & Townsend is a global professional services company with over 22,000 people in more than 60 countries. 
Working with our clients across real estate, infrastructure, energy and natural resources, we transform together delivering outcomes that improve people’s lives. Working in partnership makes it possible to deliver the world’s most impactful projects and programmes as we turn challenge into opportunity and complexity into success. 
Our capabilities include programme, project, cost, asset and commercial management, controls and performance, procurement and supply chain, net zero and digital solutions. 
We are majority-owned by CBRE Group, Inc., the world’s largest commercial real estate services and investment firm, with our partners holding a significant minority interest. Turner & Townsend and CBRE work together to provide clients with the premier programme, project and cost management offering in markets around the world. 

Turner & Townsend 
is seeking a 
Senior Construction Scheduler 
to work with our team in 
Dallas
, 
TX
 and a leading technology client on a large-scale data center construction program.
The Senior Scheduler should have experience working with cross-functional teams and stakeholders to plan, develop and execute construction schedules for mission critical facilities. This includes new-builds and retrofits to existing /operating facilities.
The ideal candidate should have an excellent understanding of scheduling best practices, resource & cost loaded scheduling, overall construction project controls as well as the interpersonal skills to be able to work closely with the internal stakeholders of the project team on a daily basis.
The Senior Scheduler will take responsibility for end to end service delivery and to act as key, day to day client interface, ensuring that client objectives are met through the delivery of a value added service. To be successful in this role you must have great communication skills and be comfortable operating in a client-facing role.
Responsibilities:
Regular travel to construction site is expected.
Effectively work with Stakeholders, Clients, Contractors and Sub Contractors on a daily basis.
Develop and maintain a detailed construction program schedule using Primavera P6 and Tableau for multi-project environments.
Ensure that schedule related data from vendors, suppliers, engineering and construction contractors of actual projects is provided as feedback into the planning and scheduling systems.
Implement Project Planning & Scheduling strategy, plans and procedures, reflecting both Company and contractor roles, responsibilities and expectations.
Actively work with project managers, construction firms and subcontractor firms as necessary to maintain schedule integrity.
Provide interface and quality assurance to Project functional groups and contractors regarding the tracking and reporting of schedule performance.
Ability to coordinate & organize multiple sources of schedule inputs/performance data into a master schedule platform and deliver project/program status reports as required.
Prepare and update progress reports as required by the client, including the Integrated Planning / Scheduling contribution to the monthly project report and specific reports / presentations.
Produce high level and 1, 3, 6 month look ahead from P6 for reporting.
Perform probabilistic analysis on integrated schedules and contractor schedules.
Actively monitor and communicate any possible project issues that could delay the schedule.
Conduct the required project schedule analysis, critical path analysis and schedule risk analysis for the project as a whole.
Analyze deviations from the baseline in the Project Master schedule highlighting bottlenecks / delays and propose corrective actions, and highlight the overall schedule impact of any variance / change order.
*SOX control responsibilities may be part of this role, which are to be adhered to where applicable.

Experience working in mission critical environments is preferred including commissioning activities.
Construction experience- i.e. “boots on the ground.” This is site-level construction experience who knows the construction process.
Understanding of best practice relating to the delivery of a construction program is required.
Extensive experience creating and managing large-scale construction schedules in Primavera P6.
A background in Project Controls is beneficial.
Familiarity with construction drawings, specifications and construction sequencing is required.
Being able to work independently is crucial.
Capable of producing detailed concept level schedules from limited project information. Identifying major phases through that timeline and be able to determine and discuss dependencies.

Knowledge of system start-up sequences and major dependencies.
Able to convert data into Tableau reports and graphics.
Excellent collaboration and communication skills are required.
BS Degree in Engineering or Business or related field; or demonstrated equivalent and related experience.
PSP certification by AACE in planning/scheduling is beneficial.
EIT certification Preferred.

Project Overview:
 
Bechtel is partnering with NextDecade to support their vision to provide the world access to lower carbon intensive energy with their Rio Grande LNG (RGLNG) project in Brownsville, Texas.
RGLNG is a natural gas liquefaction and export terminal situated on a 984-acre site on the banks of the Brownsville ship channel. The first phase of the RGLNG project consists of three liquefaction trains, two storage tanks and one marine berth. At full capacity, the five-train facility will have a production capacity of 27 million tonnes per annum (MTPA).
Brownsville, Texas is a city known for its diverse history, tradition, and rich culture. Located in the southernmost region in the beautiful state of Texas, lays Brownsville a rich, tropical oasis bordering the Rio Grande River and near the shores of the Gulf of Mexico. Brownsville embraces innovation, looks forward to the future and beyond!
Job Summary:
 
This position will be responsible to provide leadership and coordination for planning and execution of simultaneous operations (SIMOPS) during construction, pre-commissioning, commissioning, and startup phases. Ensure hazards are identified, risks assessed, and mitigation measures implemented in accordance with SIMOPS procedure to protect personnel, facilities, and environment.#LI-SP1
Major Responsibilities:
 
Assesses and verifies the integrity of mechanical systems during Installation, Commissioning, and Startup, to maximize system reliability and availability, by carrying out inspections and construction support as needed.
Provide ES&H leadership to personnel assigned to them.
Complete testing per STCP’s, SWPP’s, project procedures and other specific procedures which may be required to be prepared in this position. Complete all test records, data sheets, etc. to fully document testing activities
Ensures that Bechtel and local/national safety codes, requirements and standards are being complied with within assigned area of responsibility. 
Actively participates in safety programs.
Receives administrative supervision and technical guidance from the OSBL Area Lead. Objectives are defined, and results are subject to supervisory review. 
Provides technical guidance and assigns work to project Commissioning and Startup, technicians, crafts, and others who are performing specific assignments.
Coordinates between project engineering, construction, specialty staff groups, clients, and vendors.
Prepare FCR/NCR/DR’s as required to document as-built conditions and/or properly resolve deficiencies
Plans, schedules, conducts, or coordinates detailed CSU activities or maintenance, including reviews for safety and execution.
Performs work involving conventional practice but may include complex features such as conflicting priorities, unsuitability of conventional methods, or difficult coordination requirements.
Other Responsibilities
 
Ensure permanent plant materials are stored in accordance with specifications and project requirements. Responsible for testing of mechanical system(s) as per supplier and code requirements.
Participate in system turnover walkdowns, both Construction and Client turnovers; initiate, track and resolve punchlist items for assigned areas of responsibility
Prepares and Maintains Mechanical Spares for Commissioning and startup. Monitors Commissioning & Startup spares usage on the site and Prepares Field Material Requisitions for permanent plant material to ensure that the CSU activities to be productive.
Responsible for onsite activities of subcontractors, suppliers, clients and their representatives and others as may be assigned within area of responsibility.
Preparing reports and forecasts, including summary of CSU progress and craft personnel forecast.
Monitors the activities of subcontractors to ensure compliance with specifications and schedules.

University/B.S degree in Mechanical Engineering plus 6 years of experience or 10 years of equivalent industry experience in-lieu of a degree.

Heavy industrial direct hire construction experience in a supervisory role commensurate with the type of work to be undertaken, preferably in a lump-sum turn-key environment.
The ideal candidate possesses extensive and a broad technical experience of commissioning, startup, operation, maintenance, and testing of Mechanical/Piping Systems/Components of Oil & Gas Processing Facilities.
Good Knowledge and Understanding of engineering systems, applications of startup and operations; and previous experience in Mechanical Commissioning roles.

Good knowledge in MS Word, Excel, Visio, PowerPoint, and other relevant Bechtel used applications (Aconex, Set Route).
Understands project workflows from design, estimation, construction administration and coordination, and fabrication.

Experience in the design of LNG facilities.
Understanding of applicable Bechtel work processes including Standard Work Process Procedures.
Familiarity with Bechtel Standard Applications (BSAPs) including Setroute, Unifier, Aconex, DSCS, PTR, Agile, Navisworks, and other automation tools which are used on Bechtel projects.
Strong supervision experience including the ability to lead and manage change.
